color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 28px; margin: 0px 0px 0px 48px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">Ans- The excessive use of pesticides affects the nervous system and can cause impotence, liver and kidney dysfunction. They can also cause disabilities, miscarriage and skin, heart and eye ailments.</span></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 28px; margin: 0px 0px 0px 48px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; text-indent: -0.25in; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">h.<span style="font-family: "Times New Roman"; font-size: 7pt; font-stretch: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; line-height: normal; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">    </span></span></span><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">Who will be disproportionately affected by climate change?</span></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 28px; margin: 0px 0px 0px 48px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">Ans- The poor will be disproportionately affected by climate change.</span></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 28px; margin: 0px 0px 0px 48px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; text-indent: -0.25in; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">i.<span style="font-family: "Times New Roman"; font-size: 7pt; font-stretch: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; line-height: normal; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">      </span></span></span><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">Who amended Regional Integrated model of Climate and the Economy?</span></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 28px; margin: 0px 0px 0px 48px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">Ans- Francis Denning and his colleagues developed Regional Integrated Model of Climate and the Economy.</span></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 28px; margin: 0px 0px 0px 48px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; text-indent: -0.25in; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">j.<span style="font-family: "Times New Roman"; font-size: 7pt; font-stretch: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; line-height: normal; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">      </span></span></span><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">Why was Regional Integrated model of Climate and the Economy developed?</span></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 28px; margin: 0px 0px 0px 48px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">Ans- Regional Integrated Model of Climate and the Economy was developed to study the inequalities within different regions of the world essentially acknowledging that different countries contain people of both higher and lower incomes.</span></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div align="center" style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 28px; margin: 0px 0px 0px 48px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; text-align: center; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><h2 style="color: #2c3e50; font-family: "PT Sans Narrow", sans-serif; font-weight: 400; margin: 0px 0px 15px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; position: relative; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><b style="outline: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">Unit-8</span></b></h2><h2 style="color: #2c3e50; font-family: "PT Sans Narrow", sans-serif; font-weight: 400; margin: 0px 0px 15px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; position: relative; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><b style="outline: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">Human Trafficking</span></b></h2></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 28px; margin: 0px 0px 0px 48px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; text-indent: -0.25in; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">a.<span style="font-family: "Times New Roman"; font-size: 7pt; font-stretch: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; line-height: normal; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">    </span></span></span><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">What do you mean by human trafficking?</span></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 28px; margin: 0px 0px 0px 48px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">Ans- Human trafficking is an illegal trade of human beings for sexual exploitation, forced labour, extraction of organs or tissue and so on.</span></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 28px; margin: 0px 0px 0px 48px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; text-indent: -0.25in; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">b.<span style="font-family: "Times New Roman"; font-size: 7pt; font-stretch: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; line-height: normal; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">    </span></span></span><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">Who is prone to trafficking?</span></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 28px; margin: 0px 0px 0px 48px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">Ans- People from low-income households, ethnic minorities, illiterate or people with low level education, refugees, illegal migrants, children running away from home, members of split families, women of forced marriage and early marriage, deserted wife, widows and discriminated daughters are prone to trafficking.</span></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 28px; margin: 0px 0px 0px 48px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; text-indent: -0.25in; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">c.<span style="font-family: "Times New Roman"; font-size: 7pt; font-stretch: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; line-height: normal; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">    </span></span></span><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">How do traffickers victimise the targeted people?</span></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 28px; margin: 0px 0px 0px 48px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">Ans- Traffickers victimize the targeted people as they are provided with economic incentive and financial loans and lured to promises of better jobs or well-paid job in cities, false marriages and proposals, easy money, the dream of sophisticated life and other.</span></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 28px; margin: 0px 0px 0px 48px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; text-indent: -0.25in; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">d.<span style="font-family: "Times New Roman"; font-size: 7pt; font-stretch: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; line-height: normal; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">    </span></span></span><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">Human trafficking is another form of slavery. Do you agree or disagree? Explain why.</span></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 28px; margin: 0px 0px 0px 48px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">Ans- Yes, I agree that human trafficking is another form of slavery. <span style="color: black; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">Most victims are involved in slavery like practices, and kept in prison like<span style="margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"> </span></span><span style="color: black; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">environment. It is because they can be physically and sexually abused. They<span style="margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"> </span></span><span style="color: black; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">have to work long hours without any rest or recreation. They never get medical<span style="margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"> </span></span><span style="color: black; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">facility when they fall sick. They are either paid less. </span><br style="outline: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;" /></span></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 28px; margin: 0px 0px 0px 48px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; text-indent: -0.25in; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">e.<span style="font-family: "Times New Roman"; font-size: 7pt; font-stretch: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; line-height: normal; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">    </span></span></span><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">‘Unlike common people, victims’ life is different.’ Justify it with an example.</span></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 28px; margin: 0px 0px 0px 48px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">Ans- Common people have their own way of life, but the victims are compelled to live the life decided by others. For example, a domestic servant has to work according to the demand of his/her master. He/she is not given any chance to fulfill his/her desires.</span></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div align="center" style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 28px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; text-align: center; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><h2 style="color: #2c3e50; font-family: "PT Sans Narrow", sans-serif; font-weight: 400; margin: 0px 0px 15px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; position: relative; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><b style="outline: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; position: relative; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><b style="outline: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">The Road Not Taken</span></b></h2></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 28px; margin: 0px 0px 0px 48px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; text-indent: -0.25in; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">a.<span style="font-family: "Times New Roman"; font-size: 7pt; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">b.<span style="font-family: "Times New Roman"; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">Where is the speaker standing in this poem?</span></div><div style="background-color: white; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">Ans- An infectious disease is a disease caused by the entrance of pathogenic microorganism such as bacteria, virus, parasites, fungi etc. into the human body.</span></div><div style="background-color: white; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">Who composed this poem?</span></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">Ans- Thomas Hood composed this poem.</span></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">Ans- The poem is about the childhood memories of the poet which he compares with his adulthood.</span></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">What does the poet remember in the first stanza?</span></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">Ans- The poet remembers the house where he was born and the little window through which the sun rays entered his house.</span></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">What does he wish in the first stanza?</span></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">Ans- He wishes that the night would take his breath away.</span></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">Ans- He remembers red and white roses, violets, lily-cups, robin and laburnum.</span></div><div style="background-color: white; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 28px; margin: 0px 0px 0px 48px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; text-indent: -0.25in; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">How does the poet describe his childhood in the third stanza?</span></div><div style="background-color: white; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">Ans- The poet used to swing, enjoy the breeze. Also, he was all energetic and high in spirit.</span></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 28px; margin: 0px 0px 0px 48px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; text-indent: -0.25in; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">g.<span style="font-family: "Times New Roman"; font-size: 7pt; font-stretch: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; line-height: normal; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">    </span></span></span><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">Was the poet really closer to the heaven when he was a child? Why does he think so?</span></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 28px; margin: 0px 0px 0px 48px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">Ans- No, the poet was not really closer to the heaven when he was a child. But he thinks he was closer to the heaven because of his childish ignorance.</span></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div align="center" style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-weight: 400; margin: 0px 0px 15px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; position: relative; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><b style="outline: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">Jitiya Festival</span></b></h2></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 28px; margin: 0px 0px 0px 48px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; text-indent: -0.25in; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">h.<span style="font-family: "Times New Roman"; font-size: 7pt; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">Why is Jitiya festival celebrated?</span></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 28px; margin: 0px 0px 0px 48px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">Ans- Jitiya festival is celebrated for the good fortune and long life for the husband and children by married women.</span></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 28px; margin: 0px 0px 0px 48px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; text-indent: -0.25in; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">i.<span style="font-family: "Times New Roman"; font-size: 7pt; font-stretch: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; line-height: normal; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">      </span></span></span><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">How long is this festival celebrated?</span></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 28px; margin: 0px 0px 0px 48px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">Ans- This festival is celebrated for three days.</span></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">j.<span style="font-family: "Times New Roman"; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">What do married women do on the second day of celebration?</span></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 28px; margin: 0px 0px 0px 48px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">Ans- On the second day, the married women fast the whole day. They go to the river, pond and well and make an idol of Jimutavahana made of kush (the holy grass), and worship the idol. The devotees get together and the ones who know about Jimutavahana, narrate his story. During fasting hours, they sing and dance, too.</span></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 28px; margin: 0px 0px 0px 48px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; text-indent: -0.25in; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">k.<span style="font-family: "Times New Roman"; font-size: 7pt; font-stretch: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; line-height: normal; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">    </span></span></span><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">How and when do married women scrub their house?</span></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 28px; margin: 0px 0px 0px 48px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">Ans- On the first day of the celebration, women scrub their house with cow’s dung to make their house sacred.</span></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 28px; margin: 0px 0px 0px 48px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; text-indent: -0.25in; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 7pt; font-stretch: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; line-height: normal; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">      </span></span></span><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">What is the relationship between Masabashi and the Sun?</span></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 28px; margin: 0px 0px 0px 48px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 32px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;">Ans- Masabashi’s son named Jimutavahana was a blessing son of the Sun.</span></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"></div><div style="background-color: white; color: #151515; font-family: "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 28px; margin: 0px 0px 0px 48px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; text-indent: -0.25in; transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;"><span style="font-family: arial, sans-serif;
